[<span data-ttu-id="a6388-105">Instalar o pacote de hospedagem do .NET Core</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-105">Install the .NET Core Hosting Bundle</span></span>](#install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle)

## <a name="supported-operating-systems"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-106">Sistemas operacionais com suporte</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-106">Supported operating systems</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-107">Há suporte para os seguintes sistemas operacionais:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-107">The following operating systems are supported:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6388-108">Windows 7 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-108">Windows 7 or later</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a6388-109">Windows Server 2012 R2 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-109">Windows Server 2012 R2 or later</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-110">O [servidor HTTP.sys](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (anteriormente chamado de WebListener) não funciona em uma configuração de proxy reverso com o IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-110">[HTTP.sys server](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (formerly called WebListener) doesn't work in a reverse proxy configuration with IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-111">Use o [servidor Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-111">Use the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-112">Para obter mais informações sobre hospedagem no Azure, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-112">For information on hosting in Azure, see <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-113">Para obter as diretrizes de solução de problemas, consulte <xref:test/troubleshoot>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-113">For troubleshooting guidance, see <xref:test/troubleshoot>.</span></span>

## <a name="supported-platforms"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-114">Plataformas com Suporte</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-114">Supported platforms</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-115">Aplicativos publicados para implantação de 32 bits (x86) ou 64 bits (x64) têm suporte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-115">Apps published for 32-bit (x86) or 64-bit (x64) deployment are supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-116">Implantar um aplicativo de 32 bits com um SDK do .NET Core de 32 bits (x86), a menos que o aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-116">Deploy a 32-bit app with a 32-bit (x86) .NET Core SDK unless the app:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6388-117">Exija o maior espaço de endereço de memória virtual disponível para um aplicativo de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-117">Requires the larger virtual memory address space available to a 64-bit app.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a6388-118">Exija o maior tamanho de pilha do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-118">Requires the larger IIS stack size.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a6388-119">Tenha dependências nativas de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-119">Has 64-bit native dependencies.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-120">Use um SDK do .NET Core de 64 bits (x64) para publicar um aplicativo de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-120">Use a 64-bit (x64) .NET Core SDK to publish a 64-bit app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-121">Um runtime de 64 bits deve estar presente no sistema host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-121">A 64-bit runtime must be present on the host system.</span></span>

## <a name="hosting-models"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-122">Modelos de hospedagem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-122">Hosting models</span></span>

### <a name="in-process-hosting-model"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-123">Modelo de hospedagem em processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-123">In-process hosting model</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-124">Usando uma hospedagem em processo, um aplicativo ASP.NET Core é executado no mesmo processo que seu processo de trabalho do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-124">Using in-process hosting, an ASP.NET Core app runs in the same process as its IIS worker process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-125">A hospedagem em processo oferece desempenho melhor em hospedagem fora do processo porque as solicitações não são transmitidas por proxy pelo adaptador de loopback, um adaptador de rede que retorna o tráfego de rede de saída para o mesmo computador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-125">In-process hosting provides improved performance over out-of-process hosting because requests aren't proxied over the loopback adapter, a network interface that returns outgoing network traffic back to the same machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-126">O IIS manipula o gerenciamento de processos com o [WAS (Serviço de Ativação de Processos do Windows)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-126">IIS handles process management with the [Windows Process Activation Service (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-127">O [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-127">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module):</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6388-128">Executa a inicialização do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-128">Performs app initialization.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="a6388-129">Carrega o [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-129">Loads the [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr).</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="a6388-130">Chama `Program.Main`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-130">Calls `Program.Main`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a6388-131">Manipula o tempo de vida da solicitação nativa do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-131">Handles the lifetime of the IIS native request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-132">Não há suporte para o modelo de hospedagem em processo para aplicativos ASP.NET Core direcionados ao .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-132">The in-process hosting model isn't supported for ASP.NET Core apps that target the .NET Framework.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-133">O diagrama a seguir ilustra a relação entre o IIS, o Módulo do ASP.NET Core e um aplicativo hospedado em processo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-133">The following diagram illustrates the relationship between IIS, the ASP.NET Core Module, and an app hosted in-process:</span></span>

![Módulo do ASP.NET Core no cenário de hospedagem em processo](index/_static/ancm-inprocess.png)

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-135">A solicitação chega da Web para o driver do HTTP.sys no modo kernel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-135">A request arrives from the web to the kernel-mode HTTP.sys driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-136">O driver roteia as solicitações nativas ao IIS na porta configurada do site, normalmente, a 80 (HTTP) ou a 443 (HTTPS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-136">The driver routes the native request to IIS on the website's configured port, usually 80 (HTTP) or 443 (HTTPS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-137">O módulo ASP.NET Core recebe a solicitação nativa e a passa para o servidor HTTP IIS`IISHttpServer`().</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-137">The ASP.NET Core Module receives the native request and passes it to IIS HTTP Server (`IISHttpServer`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-138">O servidor HTTP do IIS é uma implementação de servidor em processo do IIS que converte a solicitação de nativa para gerenciada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-138">IIS HTTP Server is an in-process server implementation for IIS that converts the request from native to managed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-139">Depois que o Servidor HTTP do IIS processa a solicitação, a solicitação é enviada por push para o pipeline de middleware do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-139">After the IIS HTTP Server processes the request, the request is pushed into the ASP.NET Core middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-140">O pipeline do middleware manipula a solicitação e a passa como uma instância de `HttpContext` para a lógica do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-140">The middleware pipeline handles the request and passes it on as an `HttpContext` instance to the app's logic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-141">A resposta do aplicativo é retornada ao IIS por meio do Servidor HTTP do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-141">The app's response is passed back to IIS through IIS HTTP Server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-142">O IIS enviará a resposta ao cliente que iniciou a solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-142">IIS sends the response to the client that initiated the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-143">A hospedagem em processo é uma opção de aceitação para os aplicativos existentes, mas o padrão dos modelos [dotnet new](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-new) é o modelo de hospedagem em processo para todos os cenários do IIS e do IIS Express.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-143">In-process hosting is opt-in for existing apps, but [dotnet new](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-new) templates default to the in-process hosting model for all IIS and IIS Express scenarios.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-144">`CreateDefaultBuilder` adiciona uma instância <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.Server.IServer> chamando o método <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIIS*> para inicializar o [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr) e hospedar o aplicativo no processo de trabalho do IIS (*w3wp.exe* ou *iisexpress.exe*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-144">`CreateDefaultBuilder` adds an <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.Server.IServer> instance by calling the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIIS*> method to boot the [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr) and host the app inside of the IIS worker process (*w3wp.exe* or *iisexpress.exe*).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-145">Os testes de desempenho indicam que hospedar um aplicativo em processo do .NET Core oferece uma taxa de transferência de solicitação significativamente mais elevada em comparação a hospedar o aplicativo fora do processo e enviar por proxy as solicitações para o servidor [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-145">Performance tests indicate that hosting a .NET Core app in-process delivers significantly higher request throughput compared to hosting the app out-of-process and proxying requests to [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) server.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-146">Aplicativos publicados como um único arquivo executável não podem ser carregados pelo modelo de hospedagem em processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-146">Apps published as a single file executable can't be loaded by the in-process hosting model.</span></span>

### <a name="out-of-process-hosting-model"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-147">Modelo de hospedagem de fora do processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-147">Out-of-process hosting model</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-148">Como ASP.NET Core aplicativos são executados em um processo separado do processo de trabalho do IIS, o módulo ASP.NET Core lida com o gerenciamento de processos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-148">Because ASP.NET Core apps run in a process separate from the IIS worker process, the ASP.NET Core Module handles process management.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-149">O módulo inicia o processo para o aplicativo ASP.NET Core quando a primeira solicitação chega e reinicia o aplicativo se ele é desligado ou falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-149">The module starts the process for the ASP.NET Core app when the first request arrives and restarts the app if it shuts down or crashes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-150">Isso é basicamente o mesmo comportamento que o dos aplicativos que são executados dentro do processo e são gerenciados pelo [WAS (Serviço de Ativação de Processos do Windows)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-150">This is essentially the same behavior as seen with apps that run in-process that are managed by the [Windows Process Activation Service (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-151">O diagrama a seguir ilustra a relação entre o IIS, o Módulo do ASP.NET Core e um aplicativo hospedado de fora d processo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-151">The following diagram illustrates the relationship between IIS, the ASP.NET Core Module, and an app hosted out-of-process:</span></span>

![Módulo do ASP.NET Core no cenário de hospedagem fora do processo](index/_static/ancm-outofprocess.png)

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-153">As solicitações chegam da Web para o driver do HTTP.sys no modo kernel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-153">Requests arrive from the web to the kernel-mode HTTP.sys driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-154">O driver roteia as solicitações ao IIS na porta configurada do site, normalmente, a 80 (HTTP) ou a 443 (HTTPS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-154">The driver routes the requests to IIS on the website's configured port, usually 80 (HTTP) or 443 (HTTPS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-155">O módulo encaminha as solicitações ao Kestrel em uma porta aleatória do aplicativo, que não seja a porta 80 ou 443.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-155">The module forwards the requests to Kestrel on a random port for the app, which isn't port 80 or 443.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-156">O módulo especifica a porta por meio de uma variável de ambiente na inicialização e a extensão <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration*> configura o servidor para escutar em `http://localhost:{PORT}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-156">The module specifies the port via an environment variable at startup, and the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration*> extension configures the server to listen on `http://localhost:{PORT}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-157">Outras verificações são executadas e as solicitações que não se originam do módulo são rejeitadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-157">Additional checks are performed, and requests that don't originate from the module are rejected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-158">O módulo não é compatível com encaminhamento de HTTPS, portanto, as solicitações são encaminhadas por HTTP, mesmo se recebidas pelo IIS por HTTPS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-158">The module doesn't support HTTPS forwarding, so requests are forwarded over HTTP even if received by IIS over HTTPS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-159">Depois que o Kestrel coleta a solicitação do módulo, a solicitação é enviada por push ao pipeline do middleware do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-159">After Kestrel picks up the request from the module, the request is pushed into the ASP.NET Core middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-160">O pipeline do middleware manipula a solicitação e a passa como uma instância de `HttpContext` para a lógica do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-160">The middleware pipeline handles the request and passes it on as an `HttpContext` instance to the app's logic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-161">O middleware adicionado pela integração do IIS atualiza o esquema, o IP remoto e pathbase para encaminhar a solicitação para o Kestrel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-161">Middleware added by IIS Integration updates the scheme, remote IP, and pathbase to account for forwarding the request to Kestrel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-162">A resposta do aplicativo é retornada ao IIS, que a retorna por push para o cliente HTTP que iniciou a solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-162">The app's response is passed back to IIS, which pushes it back out to the HTTP client that initiated the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-163">Para orientação sobre a configuração do Módulo do ASP.NET Core, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-163">For ASP.NET Core Module configuration guidance, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-164">Para saber mais sobre hospedagem, confira [Host no ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-164">For more information on hosting, see [Host in ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span></span>

## <a name="application-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-165">Configuração de aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-165">Application configuration</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-iisintegration-components"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-166">Habilitar os componentes de IISIntegration</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-166">Enable the IISIntegration components</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-167">Ao criar um host no `CreateHostBuilder` (*Program.cs*), chame <xref:Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting.Host.CreateDefaultBuilder*> para habilitar a integração do IIS:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-167">When building a host in `CreateHostBuilder` (*Program.cs*), call <xref:Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting.Host.CreateDefaultBuilder*> to enable IIS integration:</span></span>

```csharp
public static IHostBuilder CreateHostBuilder(string[] args) =>
    Host.CreateDefaultBuilder(args)
        ...
```

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-168">Para obter mais informações sobre o `CreateDefaultBuilder`, consulte <xref:fundamentals/host/generic-host#default-builder-settings>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-168">For more information on `CreateDefaultBuilder`, see <xref:fundamentals/host/generic-host#default-builder-settings>.</span></span>

### <a name="iis-options"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-169">Opções do IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-169">IIS options</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-170">**Modelo de hospedagem em processo**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-170">**In-process hosting model**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-171">Para configurar as opções do Servidor IIS, inclua uma configuração de serviço para <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISServerOptions> em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-171">To configure IIS Server options, include a service configuration for <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISServerOptions> in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-172">O exemplo a seguir desabilita AutomaticAuthentication:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-172">The following example disables AutomaticAuthentication:</span></span>

```csharp
services.Configure<IISServerOptions>(options => 
{
    options.AutomaticAuthentication = false;
});
```

| <span data-ttu-id="a6388-173">Opção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-173">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="a6388-174">Padrão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-174">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a6388-175">Setting</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-175">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="a6388-176">Se `true`, o Servidor do IIS define o `HttpContext.User` autenticado pela [Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-176">If `true`, IIS Server sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-177">Se `false`, o servidor fornecerá apenas uma identidade para `HttpContext.User` e responderá a desafios quando explicitamente solicitado pelo `AuthenticationScheme`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-177">If `false`, the server only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-178">A autenticação do Windows deve estar habilitada no IIS para que o `AutomaticAuthentication` funcione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-178">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-179">Para obter mais informações, veja [Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-179">For more information, see [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="a6388-180">Configura o nome de exibição mostrado aos usuários em páginas de logon.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-180">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |
| `AllowSynchronousIO`           | `false` | <span data-ttu-id="a6388-181">Se a e/s síncrona é permitida para `HttpContext.Request` o e `HttpContext.Response`o.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-181">Whether synchronous I/O is allowed for the `HttpContext.Request` and the `HttpContext.Response`.</span></span> |
| `MaxRequestBodySize`           | `30000000`  | <span data-ttu-id="a6388-182">Obtém ou define o tamanho máximo do corpo da solicitação para o `HttpRequest`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-182">Gets or sets the max request body size for the `HttpRequest`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-183">Observe que o próprio IIS tem o limite `maxAllowedContentLength` que será processado antes de `MaxRequestBodySize` definido no `IISServerOptions`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-183">Note that IIS itself has the limit `maxAllowedContentLength` which will be processed before the `MaxRequestBodySize` set in the `IISServerOptions`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-184">Alterar `MaxRequestBodySize` não afetará `maxAllowedContentLength`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-184">Changing the `MaxRequestBodySize` won't affect the `maxAllowedContentLength`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-185">Para aumentar `maxAllowedContentLength`, adicione uma entrada em *web.config* para definir `maxAllowedContentLength` para um valor mais alto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-185">To increase `maxAllowedContentLength`, add an entry in the *web.config* to set `maxAllowedContentLength` to a higher value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-186">Para obter mais detalhes, confira [Configuração](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/requestFiltering/requestLimits/#configuration).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-186">For more details, see [Configuration](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/requestFiltering/requestLimits/#configuration).</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-187">**Modelo de hospedagem de fora do processo**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-187">**Out-of-process hosting model**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-188">Para configurar opções do IIS, inclua uma configuração de serviço para <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-188">To configure IIS options, include a service configuration for <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-189">O exemplo a seguir impede que o aplicativo preencha `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-189">The following example prevents the app from populating `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.Configure<IISOptions>(options => 
{
    options.ForwardClientCertificate = false;
});
```

| <span data-ttu-id="a6388-190">Opção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-190">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="a6388-191">Padrão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-191">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a6388-192">Setting</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-192">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="a6388-193">Se `true`, o [middleware de integração do IIS](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) define o `HttpContext.User` autenticado pela [Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-193">If `true`, [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-194">Se `false`, o middleware fornecerá apenas uma identidade para `HttpContext.User` e responderá a desafios quando explicitamente solicitado pelo `AuthenticationScheme`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-194">If `false`, the middleware only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-195">A autenticação do Windows deve estar habilitada no IIS para que o `AutomaticAuthentication` funcione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-195">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-196">Saiba mais no tópico [Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-196">For more information, see the [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth) topic.</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="a6388-197">Configura o nome de exibição mostrado aos usuários em páginas de logon.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-197">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |
| `ForwardClientCertificate`     | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="a6388-198">Se `true` e o cabeçalho da solicitação `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` estiverem presentes, o `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate` será populado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-198">If `true` and the `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` request header is present, the `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate` is populated.</span></span> |

### <a name="proxy-server-and-load-balancer-scenarios"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-199">Servidor proxy e cenários de balanceador de carga</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-199">Proxy server and load balancer scenarios</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-200">O [Middleware de integração do IIS](#enable-the-iisintegration-components), que configura o Middleware de cabeçalhos encaminhados, e o módulo do ASP.NET Core, são configurados para encaminhar o esquema (HTTP/HTTPS) e o endereço IP remoto de onde a solicitação foi originada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-200">The [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components), which configures Forwarded Headers Middleware, and the ASP.NET Core Module are configured to forward the scheme (HTTP/HTTPS) and the remote IP address where the request originated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-201">Configuração adicional pode ser necessária para aplicativos hospedados atrás de servidores proxy adicionais e balanceadores de carga.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-201">Additional configuration might be required for apps hosted behind additional proxy servers and load balancers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-202">Para obter mais informações, veja [Configurar o ASP.NET Core para trabalhar com servidores proxy e balanceadores de carga](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-202">For more information, see [Configure ASP.NET Core to work with proxy servers and load balancers](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer).</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-203">Arquivo web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-203">web.config file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-204">O arquivo *web.config* configura o [Módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-204">The *web.config* file configures the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-205">Criando, transformar e publicar o arquivo *Web.config* é tratado por um destino do MSBuild (`_TransformWebConfig`) quando o projeto é publicado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-205">Creating, transforming, and publishing the *web.config* file is handled by an MSBuild target (`_TransformWebConfig`) when the project is published.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-206">Este destino está presente nos destinos do SDK da Web (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-206">This target is present in the Web SDK targets (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-207">O SDK é definido na parte superior do arquivo de projeto:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-207">The SDK is set at the top of the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<Project Sdk="Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web">
```

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-208">Se um arquivo *web.config* não estiver presente no projeto, ele será criado com o *processPath* e os *argumentos* corretos para configurar o Módulo do ASP.NET Core e será transferido para o [resultado publicado](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-208">If a *web.config* file isn't present in the project, the file is created with the correct *processPath* and *arguments* to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to [published output](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-209">Se um arquivo *web.config* estiver presente no projeto, ele será transformado com o *processPath* e os *argumentos* corretos para configurar o Módulo do ASP.NET Core e será movido para o resultado publicado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-209">If a *web.config* file is present in the project, the file is transformed with the correct *processPath* and *arguments* to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to published output.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-210">A transformação não altera as definições de configuração do IIS no arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-210">The transformation doesn't modify IIS configuration settings in the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-211">O arquivo *web.config* pode fornecer configurações adicionais do IIS que controlam módulos ativos do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-211">The *web.config* file may provide additional IIS configuration settings that control active IIS modules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-212">Para saber mais sobre os módulos do IIS que podem processar solicitações com aplicativos do ASP.NET Core, veja o tópico [Módulos do IIS](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-212">For information on IIS modules that are capable of processing requests with ASP.NET Core apps, see the [IIS modules](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules) topic.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-213">Para impedir que o SDK Web transforme o arquivo *web.config*, use a propriedade **\<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>** no arquivo do projeto:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-213">To prevent the Web SDK from transforming the *web.config* file, use the **\<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>** property in the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<PropertyGroup>
  <IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>true</IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>
</PropertyGroup>
```

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-214">Ao impedir que o SDK Web transforme o arquivo, o *processPath* e os *argumentos* devem ser definidos manualmente pelo desenvolvedor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-214">When disabling the Web SDK from transforming the file, the *processPath* and *arguments* should be manually set by the developer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-215">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-215">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file-location"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-216">Local do arquivo web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-216">web.config file location</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-217">Para configurar o [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) corretamente, o arquivo *Web. config* deve estar presente no caminho [raiz do conteúdo](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root) (normalmente o caminho base do aplicativo) do aplicativo implantado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-217">In order to set up the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) correctly, the *web.config* file must be present at the [content root](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root) path (typically the app base path) of the deployed app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-218">Esse é o mesmo local que o caminho físico do site fornecido ao IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-218">This is the same location as the website physical path provided to IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-219">O arquivo *web.config* é necessário na raiz do aplicativo para habilitar a publicação de vários aplicativos usando a Implantação da Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-219">The *web.config* file is required at the root of the app to enable the publishing of multiple apps using Web Deploy.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-220">Existem arquivos confidenciais no caminho físico do aplicativo, como \* \<assembly>. runtimeconfig. JSON*, \* \<assembly>. xml* (comentários de documentação XML) e \* \<assembly>. deps. JSON\*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-220">Sensitive files exist on the app's physical path, such as *\<assembly>.runtimeconfig.json*, *\<assembly>.xml* (XML Documentation comments), and *\<assembly>.deps.json*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-221">Quando o arquivo *web.config* estiver presente e o site for iniciado normalmente, o IIS não atenderá a esses arquivos confidenciais se eles forem solicitados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-221">When the *web.config* file is present and the site starts normally, IIS doesn't serve these sensitive files if they're requested.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-222">Se o arquivo *web.config* estiver ausente, nomeado incorretamente ou se não for possível configurar o site para inicialização normal, o IIS poderá servir arquivos confidenciais publicamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-222">If the *web.config* file is missing, incorrectly named, or unable to configure the site for normal startup, IIS may serve sensitive files publicly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-223">**O arquivo *Web. config* deve estar presente na implantação o tempo todo, corretamente nomeado e ser capaz de configurar o site para inicialização normal. Nunca remova o arquivo *Web. config* de uma implantação de produção.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-223">**The *web.config* file must be present in the deployment at all times, correctly named, and able to configure the site for normal start up. Never remove the *web.config* file from a production deployment.**</span></span>

### <a name="transform-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-224">Transformação do Web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-224">Transform web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-225">Se você precisar transformar o *Web.config* em publicação (por exemplo, definir variáveis ​​de ambiente com base na configuração, no perfil ou no ambiente), consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-225">If you need to transform *web.config* on publish (for example, set environment variables based on the configuration, profile, or environment), see <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig>.</span></span>

## <a name="iis-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-226">Configuração do IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-226">IIS configuration</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-227">**Sistemas operacionais do Windows Server**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-227">**Windows Server operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-228">Habilite a função **Servidor Web (IIS)** e estabeleça serviços de função.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-228">Enable the **Web Server (IIS)** server role and establish role services.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-229">Use o assistente **Adicionar Funções e Recursos** por meio do menu **Gerenciar** ou do link no **Gerenciador do Servidor**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-229">Use the **Add Roles and Features** wizard from the **Manage** menu or the link in **Server Manager**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-230">Na etapa **Funções de Servidor**, marque a caixa de **Servidor Web (IIS)**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-230">On the **Server Roles** step, check the box for **Web Server (IIS)**.</span></span>

   ![A função de Servidor Web IIS é selecionada na etapa Selecionar funções de servidor.](index/_static/server-roles-ws2016.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-232">Após a etapa **Recursos**, a etapa **Serviços de função** é carregada para o servidor Web (IIS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-232">After the **Features** step, the **Role services** step loads for Web Server (IIS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-233">Selecione os serviços de função do IIS desejados ou aceite os serviços de função padrão fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-233">Select the IIS role services desired or accept the default role services provided.</span></span>

   ![Os serviços de função padrão são selecionados na etapa Selecionar serviços de função.](index/_static/role-services-ws2016.png)

   <span data-ttu-id="a6388-235">**Autenticação do Windows (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-235">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="a6388-236">Para habilitar a autenticação do Windows, expanda os seguintes nós: > **segurança**do **servidor Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-236">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Security**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-237">Selecione o recurso **Autenticação do Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-237">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-238">Saiba mais em [Autenticação do Windows \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) e [Configurar autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-238">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a6388-239">**WebSockets (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-239">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="a6388-240">O WebSockets é compatível com o ASP.NET Core 1.1 ou posterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-240">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-241">Para habilitar WebSockets, expanda os seguintes nós: > **desenvolvimento de aplicativo**de **servidor Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-241">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Application Development**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-242">Selecione o recurso **Protocolo WebSocket**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-242">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-243">Para obter mais informações, consulte [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-243">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-244">Continue para a etapa **Confirmação** para instalar os serviços e a função de servidor Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-244">Proceed through the **Confirmation** step to install the web server role and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-245">Uma reinicialização de servidor/IIS não é necessária após a instalação da função do **servidor Web (IIS)** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-245">A server/IIS restart isn't required after installing the **Web Server (IIS)** role.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-246">**Sistemas operacionais de área de trabalho do Windows**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-246">**Windows desktop operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-247">Habilite o **Console de Gerenciamento do IIS** e os **Serviços na World Wide Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-247">Enable the **IIS Management Console** and **World Wide Web Services**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-248">Navegue até **Painel de Controle** > **Programas** > **Programas e Recursos** > **Ativar ou desativar recursos do Windows** (lado esquerdo da tela).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-248">Navigate to **Control Panel** > **Programs** > **Programs and Features** > **Turn Windows features on or off** (left side of the screen).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-249">Abra o nó **Serviços de Informações da Internet**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-249">Open the **Internet Information Services** node.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-250">Abra o nó **Ferramentas de Gerenciamento da Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-250">Open the **Web Management Tools** node.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-251">Marque a caixa de **Console de Gerenciamento do IIS**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-251">Check the box for **IIS Management Console**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-252">Marque a caixa de **Serviços na World Wide Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-252">Check the box for **World Wide Web Services**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-253">Aceite os recursos padrão dos **Serviços na World Wide Web** ou personalize os recursos do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-253">Accept the default features for **World Wide Web Services** or customize the IIS features.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a6388-254">**Autenticação do Windows (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-254">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="a6388-255">Para habilitar a autenticação do Windows, expanda os seguintes nós:**segurança** **dos serviços** > de World Wide Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-255">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Security**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-256">Selecione o recurso **Autenticação do Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-256">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-257">Saiba mais em [Autenticação do Windows \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) e [Configurar autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-257">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a6388-258">**WebSockets (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-258">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="a6388-259">O WebSockets é compatível com o ASP.NET Core 1.1 ou posterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-259">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-260">Para habilitar WebSockets, expanda os seguintes nós:**recursos de desenvolvimento de aplicativos** **World Wide Web Services** > .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-260">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Application Development Features**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-261">Selecione o recurso **Protocolo WebSocket**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-261">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-262">Para obter mais informações, consulte [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-262">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-263">Se a instalação do IIS exigir uma reinicialização, reinicie o sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-263">If the IIS installation requires a restart, restart the system.</span></span>

![O Console de Gerenciamento do IIS e os Serviços na World Wide Web estão selecionados em Recursos do Windows.](index/_static/windows-features-win10.png)

## <a name="install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-265">Instalar o pacote de hospedagem do .NET Core</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-265">Install the .NET Core Hosting Bundle</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-266">Instale o *pacote de hospedagem do .NET Core* no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-266">Install the *.NET Core Hosting Bundle* on the hosting system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-267">O pacote instala o tempo de execução do .NET Core, a biblioteca do .NET Core e o [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-267">The bundle installs the .NET Core Runtime, .NET Core Library, and the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-268">O módulo permite que aplicativos do ASP.NET Core sejam executados por trás do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-268">The module allows ASP.NET Core apps to run behind IIS.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-269">Se o pacote de hospedagem for instalado antes do IIS, a instalação do pacote deverá ser reparada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-269">If the Hosting Bundle is installed before IIS, the bundle installation must be repaired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-270">Execute o instalador do pacote de hospedagem novamente depois de instalar o IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-270">Run the Hosting Bundle installer again after installing IIS.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-271">Se o pacote de hospedagem for instalado após a instalação da versão de 64 bits (x64) do .NET Core, os SDKs poderão parecer estar ausentes ([Nenhum SDK do .NET Core foi detectado](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-271">If the Hosting Bundle is installed after installing the 64-bit (x64) version of .NET Core, SDKs might appear to be missing ([No .NET Core SDKs were detected](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-272">Para resolver o problema, consulte <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-272">To resolve the problem, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-277">Para obter uma versão anterior do instalador:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-277">To obtain an earlier version of the installer:</span></span>

### <a name="install-the-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-284">Instalar o pacote de hospedagem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-284">Install the Hosting Bundle</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-285">Execute o instalador no servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-285">Run the installer on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-286">Os parâmetros a seguir estão disponíveis ao executar o instalador por meio de um shell de comando do administrador:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-286">The following parameters are available when running the installer from an administrator command shell:</span></span>

   * <span data-ttu-id="a6388-287">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1`&ndash; Ignorar a instalação do módulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-287">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1` &ndash; Skip installing the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="a6388-288">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1`&ndash; Ignorar a instalação do tempo de execução do .NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-288">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1` &ndash; Skip installing the .NET Core runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-289">Usado quando o servidor hospeda apenas [implantações independentes (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-289">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="a6388-290">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1`&ndash; Ignorar a instalação da estrutura compartilhada ASP.NET (ASP.net Runtime).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-290">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1` &ndash; Skip installing the ASP.NET Shared Framework (ASP.NET runtime).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-291">Usado quando o servidor hospeda apenas [implantações independentes (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-291">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="a6388-292">`OPT_NO_X86=1`&ndash; Ignorar a instalação de tempos de execução x86.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-292">`OPT_NO_X86=1` &ndash; Skip installing x86 runtimes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-293">Use esse parâmetro quando você souber que não hospedará aplicativos de 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-293">Use this parameter when you know that you won't be hosting 32-bit apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-294">Se houver uma possibilidade de hospedar aplicativos de 32 bits e 64 bits no futuro, não use esse parâmetro e instale ambos os runtimes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-294">If there's any chance that you will host both 32-bit and 64-bit apps in the future, don't use this parameter and install both runtimes.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="a6388-295">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1` &ndash; Desabilite a verificação para usar uma Configuração Compartilhada do IIS quando a configuração compartilhada (*applicationHost.config*) estiver no mesmo computador do que a instalação do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-295">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1` &ndash; Disable the check for using an IIS Shared Configuration when the shared configuration (*applicationHost.config*) is on the same machine as the IIS installation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-296">*Disponível somente para instaladores do ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou Hosting Bundler posterior.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-296">*Only available for ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later Hosting Bundler installers.*</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-297">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-297">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-298">Reinicie o sistema ou execute os seguintes comandos em um shell de comando:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-298">Restart the system or execute the following commands in a command shell:</span></span>

   ```console
   net stop was /y
   net start w3svc
   ```
   <span data-ttu-id="a6388-299">A reinicialização do IIS identifica uma alteração no CAMINHO do sistema, que é uma variável de ambiente, realizada pelo instalador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-299">Restarting IIS picks up a change to the system PATH, which is an environment variable, made by the installer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-300">ASP.NET Core não adota o comportamento de roll-forward para versões de patch de pacotes de estrutura compartilhados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-300">ASP.NET Core doesn't adopt roll-forward behavior for patch releases of shared framework packages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-301">Depois de atualizar a estrutura compartilhada instalando um novo pacote de hospedagem, reinicie o sistema ou execute os seguintes comandos em um shell de comando:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-301">After upgrading the shared framework by installing a new hosting bundle, restart the system or execute the following commands in a command shell:</span></span>

```console
net stop was /y
net start w3svc
```

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-302">Para obter informações sobre a Configuração Compartilhada do IIS, consulte [Módulo do ASP.NET Core com a Configuração Compartilhada do IIS](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-302">For information on IIS Shared Configuration, see [ASP.NET Core Module with IIS Shared Configuration](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration).</span></span>

## <a name="install-web-deploy-when-publishing-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-303">Instalar a Implantação da Web durante a publicação com o Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-303">Install Web Deploy when publishing with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-304">Ao implantar aplicativos para servidores com [Implantação da Web](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later), instale a versão mais recente da Implantação da Web no servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-304">When deploying apps to servers with [Web Deploy](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later), install the latest version of Web Deploy on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-305">Para instalar a Implantação da Web, use o [WebPI (Web Platform Installer)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) ou obtenha um instalador diretamente no [Centro de Download da Microsoft](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-305">To install Web Deploy, use the [Web Platform Installer (WebPI)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) or obtain an installer directly from the [Microsoft Download Center](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-306">O método preferencial é usar o WebPI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-306">The preferred method is to use WebPI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-307">O WebPI oferece uma instalação autônoma e uma configuração para provedores de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-307">WebPI offers a standalone setup and a configuration for hosting providers.</span></span>

## <a name="create-the-iis-site"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-308">Criar o site do IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-308">Create the IIS site</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-309">No sistema de hospedagem, crie uma pasta para conter arquivos e pastas publicados do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-309">On the hosting system, create a folder to contain the app's published folders and files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-310">Em uma etapa a seguir, o caminho da pasta é fornecido ao IIS como o caminho físico para o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-310">In a following step, the folder's path is provided to IIS as the physical path to the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-311">Para obter mais informações sobre o layout de arquivo e a pasta de implantação de um aplicativo, confira <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-311">For more information on an app's deployment folder and file layout, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-312">No Gerenciador do IIS, abra o nó do servidor no painel **conexões** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-312">In IIS Manager, open the server's node in the **Connections** panel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-313">Clique com botão direito do mouse na pasta **Sites**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-313">Right-click the **Sites** folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-314">Selecione **Adicionar Site** no menu contextual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-314">Select **Add Website** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-315">Forneça um **Nome do site** e defina o **Caminho físico** como a pasta de implantação do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-315">Provide a **Site name** and set the **Physical path** to the app's deployment folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-316">Forneça a configuração de **Associação** e crie o site selecionando **OK**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-316">Provide the **Binding** configuration and create the website by selecting **OK**:</span></span>

   ![Forneça o Nome do site, o caminho físico e o Nome do host na etapa Adicionar Site.](index/_static/add-website-ws2016.png)

   > [!WARNING]
   > <span data-ttu-id="a6388-318">Associações de curinga de nível superior (`http://*:80/` e `http://+:80`) **não** devem ser usadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-318">Top-level wildcard bindings (`http://*:80/` and `http://+:80`) should **not** be used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-319">Associações de curinga de nível superior podem abrir o aplicativo para vulnerabilidades de segurança.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-319">Top-level wildcard bindings can open up your app to security vulnerabilities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-320">Isso se aplica a curingas fortes e fracos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-320">This applies to both strong and weak wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-321">Use nomes de host explícitos em vez de curingas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-321">Use explicit host names rather than wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-322">Associações de curinga de subdomínio (por exemplo, `*.mysub.com`) não têm esse risco de segurança se você controlar o domínio pai completo (em vez de `*.com`, o qual é vulnerável).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-322">Subdomain wildcard binding (for example, `*.mysub.com`) doesn't have this security risk if you control the entire parent domain (as opposed to `*.com`, which is vulnerable).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-323">Veja [rfc7230 section-5.4](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4) para obter mais informações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-323">See [rfc7230 section-5.4](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4) for more information.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-324">No nó do servidor, selecione **Pools de Aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-324">Under the server's node, select **Application Pools**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-325">Clique com o botão direito do mouse no pool de aplicativos do site e selecione **Configurações Básicas** no menu contextual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-325">Right-click the site's app pool and select **Basic Settings** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-326">Na janela **Editar Pool de Aplicativos**, defina a **versão do CLR do .NET** como **Sem Código Gerenciado**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-326">In the **Edit Application Pool** window, set the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code**:</span></span>

   ![Defina Sem Código Gerenciado para a versão do CLR do .NET.](index/_static/edit-apppool-ws2016.png)

    <span data-ttu-id="a6388-328">O ASP.NET Core é executado em um processo separado e gerencia o runtime.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-328">ASP.NET Core runs in a separate process and manages the runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-329">O ASP.NET Core não depende do carregamento do CLR de Área de trabalho (CLR do .NET)&mdash;o Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) para o .NET Core é inicializado para hospedar o aplicativo no processo de trabalho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-329">ASP.NET Core doesn't rely on loading the desktop CLR (.NET CLR)&mdash;the Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) for .NET Core is booted to host the app in the worker process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-330">Definir a **versão do CLR do .NET** como **Sem Código Gerenciado** é opcional, porém recomendado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-330">Setting the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code** is optional but recommended.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-331">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou posterior*: para uma [implantação autocontida](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) de 64 bits (x64) que usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](#in-process-hosting-model), desabilite o pool de aplicativos para processos de 32 bits (x86).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-331">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later*: For a 64-bit (x64) [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) that uses the [in-process hosting model](#in-process-hosting-model), disable the app pool for 32-bit (x86) processes.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a6388-332">Na barra lateral **Ações** do Gerenciador do IIS > **Pools de Aplicativos**, selecione **Definir Padrões do Pool de Aplicativos** ou **Configurações Avançadas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-332">In the **Actions** sidebar of IIS Manager > **Application Pools**, select **Set Application Pool Defaults** or **Advanced Settings**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-333">Localize **Habilitar Aplicativos de 32 bits** e defina o valor como `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-333">Locate **Enable 32-Bit Applications** and set the value to `False`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-334">Essa configuração não afeta os aplicativos implantados para a [hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#out-of-process-hosting-model).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-334">This setting doesn't affect apps deployed for [out-of-process hosting](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#out-of-process-hosting-model).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6388-335">Confirme se a identidade do modelo de processo tem as permissões apropriadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-335">Confirm the process model identity has the proper permissions.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a6388-336">Se a identidade padrão do pool de aplicativos (**Process Model** > **identidade**do modelo de processo) for alterada de **ApplicationPoolIdentity** para outra identidade, verifique se a nova identidade tem as permissões necessárias para acessar a pasta, o banco de dados e outros recursos necessários do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-336">If the default identity of the app pool (**Process Model** > **Identity**) is changed from **ApplicationPoolIdentity** to another identity, verify that the new identity has the required permissions to access the app's folder, database, and other required resources.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-337">Por exemplo, o pool de aplicativos requer acesso de leitura e gravação às pastas nas quais o aplicativo lê e grava os arquivos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-337">For example, the app pool requires read and write access to folders where the app reads and writes files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-338">**Configuração de Autenticação do Windows (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-338">**Windows Authentication configuration (Optional)**</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="a6388-339">Para saber mais, veja [Configurar a Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-339">For more information, see [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

## <a name="deploy-the-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-340">Implantar o aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-340">Deploy the app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-341">Implante o aplicativo na pasta **caminho físico** do IIS que foi estabelecida na seção [Criar o site do IIS](#create-the-iis-site).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-341">Deploy the app to the IIS **Physical path** folder that was established in the [Create the IIS site](#create-the-iis-site) section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6388-342">[Implantação da Web](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) é o mecanismo recomendado para implantação, mas existem várias opções para mover o aplicativo da pasta *publicar* do projeto para a pasta de implantação do sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-342">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) is the recommended mechanism for deployment, but several options exist for moving the app from the project's *publish* folder to the hosting system's deployment folder.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6388-351">Use qualquer um dos vários métodos para mover o aplicativo para o sistema host, como cópia manual, [Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy), [Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy) ou [PowerShell](/powershell/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-351">Use any of several methods to move the app to the hosting system, such as manual copy, [Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy), [Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy), or [PowerShell](/powershell/).</span></span>

## <a name="browse-the-website"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6388-353">Procurar no site</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6388-353">Browse the website</span></span>
